Execute commands INSIDE the namespace to configure its networking<\n>sudo ip netns exec vm1 ip addr add 192.168.10.10/24 dev veth0<\n>sudo ip netns exec vm1 ip link set veth0 up<\n>sudo ip netns exec vm1 ip route add default via 192.168.10.1<\n><\n># 4. sudo bpftrace -e '<\n>#include <net/tcp_states.h><\n>#include <linux/ip.h><\n>#include <linux/tcp.h><\n><\n>// --- 使用宏来封装指针转换，以绕过 bpftrace 的语法限制 ---<\n>#define ip_header ( (struct iphdr *) (((struct sk_buff *)arg0)->data) )<\n>#define tcp_header ( (struct tcphdr *) ((__u8 *)ip_header + (ip_header->ihl * 4)) )<\n><\n>kprobe:netif_receive_skb<\n>/<\n>  // 在过滤器中完成所有检查，效率更高<\n>  ((struct sk_buff *)arg0)->dev->name == "eth_main" &&<\n>  ip_header->protocol == IPPROTO_TCP<\n>/<\n>{<\n>  // 在动作块中，直接使用我们定义好的宏<\n>  printf("TCP Packet on eth_main: %u -> %u ", bswap(tcp_header->source), bswap(tcp_header->dest));<\n>  <\n>  if (tcp_header->syn)  { printf("[SYN] "); }<\n>  if (tcp_header->ack)  { printf("[ACK] "); }<\n>  if (tcp_header->fin)  { printf("[FIN] "); }<\n>  if (tcp_header->rst)  { printf("[RST] "); }<\n><\n>  printf("\n");<\n>}<\n>'
sudo bpftrace -e '<\n>#include <net/tcp_states.h><\n>#include <linux/ip.h><\n>#include <linux/tcp.h><\n><\n>// --- 使用宏来封装指针转换 ---<\n>#define ip_header ( (struct iphdr *) (((struct sk_buff *)arg0)->data) )<\n>#define tcp_header ( (struct tcphdr *) ((__u8 *)ip_header + (ip_header->ihl * 4)) )<\n><\n>kprobe:netif_receive_skb<\n>// <<< 移除这里的整个 /.../ 谓词块<\n>{<\n>  // 在动作块的开头用 if 语句完成所有检查，效率同样很高<\n>  if (((struct sk_buff *)arg0)->dev->name == "eth_main" &&<\n>      ip_header->protocol == IPPROTO_TCP)<\n>  {<\n>    // 过滤通过后，执行真正的操作<\n>    printf("TCP Packet on eth_main: %u -> %u ", bswap(tcp_header->source), bswap(tcp_header->dest));<\n><\n>    if (tcp_header->syn)  { printf("[SYN] "); }<\n>    if (tcp_header->ack)  { printf("[ACK] "); }<\n>    if (tcp_header->fin)  { printf("[FIN] "); }<\n>    if (tcp_header->rst)  { printf("[RST] "); }<\n><\n>    printf("\n");<\n>  }<\n>}<\n>'
